          function selecionaTipoConteudoParaBuscaTextual() {
              //zera o que estiver marcado
              $("#searchBar .options input[type=radio]").removeAttr("checked");
              var inputRadioId = "#type-" + $("#nav").find(".on").attr("id")

              if($(inputRadioId).length > 0){
                $(inputRadioId).attr("checked", true);
              } else {
                  //default perguntas
                $("#type-nav_questions").attr("checked", true);
              }
          }

            selecionaTipoConteudoParaBuscaTextual();

				<h1>Vídeo de ciclista headbangeando viraliza</h1>
				<span class="post-comment-box"><a href="http://www.wikimetal.com.br/site/video-de-ciclista-headbangeando-viraliza/#respond" title="Comentário para Vídeo de ciclista headbangeando viraliza">0</a></span>

<div itemprop=description>
My oh my do you wanna say goodbye?<br/>To have their Kingdom, baby, tell me why?<br/>My oh my do you wanna say goodbye?<br/>To rule a Country, baby, you and I?<br/>If you were my King...<br/><br/>My oh my do you wanna say goodbye?<br/>To have their Kingdom, baby, tell me why?<br/>My oh my do you wanna say goodbye?<br/>To rule a Country, baby, you and I?<br/><br/>A little princess in a terrible mess,<br/>a kingdom alone, with no lovers confess,<br/>dreams of a prince on a tall white horse,<br/>runs like a spirit by the castle walls.<br/><br/>Gotta steal from the rich, when they don´t know I´m coming,<br/>gotta give to the poor, no time for lovin´<br/>My oh my don´t you cry, coz there is no way I´m staying,<br/>I will leave say "bye bye", I´m going my way...<br/><br/>My oh my do you wanna say goodbye?<br/>To have their Kingdom, baby, tell me why?<br/>My oh my do you wanna say goodbye?<br/>To rule a Country, baby, you and I?<br/>If you were my King...<br/>I would be your queen....<br/>If you were my King...<br/>I would be your queen....<br/><br/>Mystery deep in the royal heart,<br/>crying at night, I wanna be a part<br/>Prince O prince are you really sincere,<br/>that you one day are gonna disappear<br/><br/>Gotta steal from the rich, when they don´t know I´m coming,<br/>gotta give to the poor, no time for lovin´<br/>My oh my don´t you cry, coz there is no way I´m staying,<br/>I will leave say "bye bye", I´m going my way...<br/><br/>My oh my.<br/>My oh my.<br/>My oh my.<br/><br/>MY OH MY!<br/><br/>My oh my do you wanna say goodbye?<br/>To have their Kingdom, baby, tell me why?<br/>My oh my do you wanna say goodbye?<br/>To rule a Country, baby, you and I?<br/><br/>My oh my do you wanna say goodbye?<br/>To have their Kingdom, baby, tell me why?<br/>My oh my do you wanna say goodbye?<br/>To rule a Country, baby, you and I?<br/>If you were my King...<br/>I would be your queen....<br/>If you were my King...<br/>I would be your queen....<br/></div>
